OBJECT Codeunit 5001904 Payment Setup
{
  OBJECT-PROPERTIES
  {
    Date=09.10.09;
    Time=12:00:00;
    Version List=AR5.01;
  }
  PROPERTIES
  {
    OnRun=BEGIN
            // Creating teaching material "Normal..."
            PermanentData(SetSelection::"Update and Add");
            TextCode2(SetSelection::"Update and Add");
            Berechtigungen(SetSelection::"Update and Add");
            Bankleitzahlen(SetSelection::"Update and Add");
            PaymentCodes(SetSelection::"Update and Add");
            DirectionCode(SetSelection::"Update and Add");
            ApplicationRecognition(SetSelection::"Update and Add");
            BankInterfaces(SetSelection::Add);
            PaymentAreas(SetSelection::Add);

            // Creating No. Series
            NoSerie.INIT;
            NoSerie.VALIDATE(Code, 'DISKNO');
            NoSerie.VALIDATE(Description, 'Disk No.');
            NoSerie.VALIDATE("Default Nos.", TRUE);
            IF NoSerie.INSERT() THEN BEGIN
              NoSerieLine.INIT;
              NoSerieLine.VALIDATE("Series Code" , 'DISKNO');
              NoSerieLine."Line No." := 10000;
              NoSerieLine.VALIDATE("Starting No.", '1');
              NoSerieLine.VALIDATE("Increment-by No.", 1);
              NoSerieLine.VALIDATE(Open, TRUE);
              IF NOT NoSerieLine.INSERT THEN ;
            END;

            NoSerie.INIT;
            NoSerie.VALIDATE(Code, 'AZVKRED');
            NoSerie.VALIDATE(Description, 'ForeignSupplement');
            NoSerie.VALIDATE("Default Nos.", TRUE);
            IF NoSerie.INSERT() THEN BEGIN
              NoSerieLine.INIT;
              NoSerieLine.VALIDATE("Series Code" , 'AZVKRED');
              NoSerieLine."Line No." := 10000;
              NoSerieLine.VALIDATE("Starting No.", '1');
              NoSerieLine.VALIDATE("Increment-by No.", 1);
              NoSerieLine.VALIDATE(Open, TRUE);
              IF NOT NoSerieLine.INSERT THEN ;
            END;

            NoSerie.INIT;
            NoSerie.VALIDATE(Code, 'AZVNO');
            NoSerie.VALIDATE(Description, 'Foreign Payments No.');
            NoSerie.VALIDATE("Default Nos.", TRUE);
            IF NoSerie.INSERT() THEN BEGIN
              NoSerieLine.INIT;
              NoSerieLine.VALIDATE("Series Code" , 'AZVNO');
              NoSerieLine."Line No." := 10000;
              NoSerieLine.VALIDATE("Starting No.", '1');
              NoSerieLine.VALIDATE("Increment-by No.", 1);
              NoSerieLine.VALIDATE(Open, TRUE);
              IF NOT NoSerieLine.INSERT THEN ;
            END;

            // Assign No. Series
            PaymSetup.GET;
            PaymSetup.VALIDATE("Interior File No.", 'DISKNO');
            PaymSetup.VALIDATE("Document No. foreign vendor",'AZVKRED');
            PaymSetup.VALIDATE("Exterior File No.",'AZVNO');
            PaymSetup.VALIDATE("Max Amount for EU-Standard out",12500);
            PaymSetup.VALIDATE("Max Amount for EU-Standard Ext",50000);
            PaymSetup.VALIDATE("Paym.Type for EU-Standard",'13');
            PaymSetup.VALIDATE("Paym.Type for EU-Expresstransf",'11');
            PaymSetup.MODIFY;
          END;

  }
  CODE
  {
    VAR
      PaymentArea@1105400029 : Record 5001950;

    PROCEDURE PermanentData@1105400012(Selection@1105400000 : ' ,Only if Table is empty,Add,Update and Add');
    BEGIN
      IF Selection = Selection::"Only if Table is empty" THEN BEGIN
        IF PaymSetup.FIND('-') THEN
          EXIT;
        Mode := Mode::Ins;
      END;

      CASE Selection OF
        Selection::" " : EXIT;
        Selection::Add : Mode := Mode::Skip;
        Selection::"Update and Add" : Mode := Mode::Modify;
      END;

      CASE Mode OF
        Mode::Ins : BEGIN
          PaymSetup.INIT;
          PaymSetup."Export Path" := 'A:\';
          PaymSetup."Payment Filename" := 'DTAUS1';
          PaymSetup."Textcode Debit Item" := '05';
          PaymSetup."Textcode Credit Note" := '51';
          PaymSetup."Textcode Collect" := '04';
          PaymSetup."With Avis" := TRUE;
          PaymSetup."No. of Entries" := 7;
          PaymSetup."Multiple Journals" := TRUE;
          PaymSetup."Import Path" := 'A:\';
          PaymSetup."Autocreate bank account(cust.)" := TRUE;
          PaymSetup."Export Path AZV" := 'A:\';
          PaymSetup."Filename AZV" := 'DTAZV';
          PaymSetup."Announcement to Bundesbank" := TRUE;
          PaymSetup."Vendor Proposal" := '%9 %2 V.%3 %8 %4 ./. SK %5';
          PaymSetup."Customer Debit Proposal" := '%9 %2 V.%3 %8 %4 ./. SK %5';
          PaymSetup."Customer Payment Proposal" := '%9 %2 V.%3 %8 %4 ./. SK %5';
          PaymSetup."Foreign Payment Proposal" := '%9 %2 F.%3';
          PaymSetup."Avis Proposal" := 'LT. AVIS VOM %7';
          PaymSetup."AZV Avis Proposal" := 'AVIS FROM %7';
          PaymSetup."Max Amount for EU-Standard out" := 12000;
          PaymSetup."Max Amount for EU-Standard Ext" := 50000;
          PaymSetup."Paym.Type for EU-Standard" := '13';
          PaymSetup."Paym.Type for EU-Expresstransf" := '11';
          PaymSetup."SEPA Proposal" := '%9 %2 V.%3 %8 %4 ./. SK %5';
          PaymSetup."No. of Entries (SEPA)" := 4;
          PaymSetup.INSERT;
        END;
        Mode::Modify : BEGIN
          IF NOT PaymSetup.GET THEN
            PaymSetup.INIT;
          PaymSetup."Export Path" := 'A:\';
          PaymSetup."Payment Filename" := 'DTAUS1';
          PaymSetup."Textcode Debit Item" := '05';
          PaymSetup."Textcode Credit Note" := '51';
          PaymSetup."Textcode Collect" := '04';
          PaymSetup."With Avis" := TRUE;
          PaymSetup."No. of Entries" := 7;
          PaymSetup."Multiple Journals" := TRUE;
          PaymSetup."Import Path" := 'A:\';
          PaymSetup."Autocreate bank account(cust.)" := TRUE;
          PaymSetup."Export Path AZV" := 'A:\';
          PaymSetup."Filename AZV" := 'DTAZV';
          PaymSetup."Announcement to Bundesbank" := TRUE;
          PaymSetup."Vendor Proposal" := '%9 %2 V.%3 %8 %4 ./. SK %5';
          PaymSetup."Customer Debit Proposal" := '%9 %2 V.%3 %8 %4 ./. SK %5';
          PaymSetup."Customer Payment Proposal" := '%9 %2 V.%3 %8 %4 ./. SK %5';
          PaymSetup."Foreign Payment Proposal" := '%9 %2 F.%3';
          PaymSetup."Avis Proposal" := 'LT. AVIS VOM %7';
          PaymSetup."AZV Avis Proposal" := 'AVIS FROM %7';
          PaymSetup."Max Amount for EU-Standard out" := 12000;
          PaymSetup."Max Amount for EU-Standard Ext" := 50000;
          PaymSetup."Paym.Type for EU-Standard" := '13';
          PaymSetup."Paym.Type for EU-Expresstransf" := '11';
          PaymSetup."SEPA Proposal" := '%9 %2 V.%3 %8 %4 ./. SK %5';
          PaymSetup."No. of Entries (SEPA)" := 4;
          IF NOT PaymSetup.INSERT THEN PaymSetup.MODIFY;
        END;
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE Berechtigungen@1105400014(Selection@1105400000 : ' ,Only if Table is empty,Add,Update and Add');
    BEGIN
      Access.SETRANGE("Role ID", AccessName);
      IF Selection = Selection::"Only if Table is empty" THEN BEGIN
        IF Access.FIND('-') THEN
          EXIT;
        Mode := Mode::Ins;
      END;

      CASE Selection OF
        Selection::" " : EXIT;
        Selection::Add : Mode := Mode::Skip;
        Selection::"Update and Add" : Mode := Mode::Modify;
      END;

      Group.INIT;
      Group."Role ID" := AccessName;
      Group.Name := 'Automatischer Zahlungsverkehr';
      IF NOT Group.INSERT THEN;

      InsertRights(0,5001901,1,1,1,1,1);

    PROCEDURE PaymentCodes@1105400016(Selection@1105400000 : ' ,Only if Table is empty,Add,Update and Add');
    BEGIN
      IF Selection = Selection::"Only if Table is empty" THEN BEGIN
        IF PaymentType.FIND('-') THEN
          EXIT;
        Mode := Mode::Ins;
      END;

      CASE Selection OF
        Selection::" " : EXIT;
        Selection::Add : Mode := Mode::Skip;
        Selection::"Update and Add" : Mode := Mode::Modify;
      END;

      InsertPaymentType('00','StandardÅbermittlung (z.B. SWIFT-Normal)',FALSE);
      InsertPaymentType('10','Telex-Zahlung oder SWIFT-Eilig',FALSE);
      InsertPaymentType('11','Taggleiche EilÅberweisung in Euro',FALSE);
      InsertPaymentType('13','EU-StandardÅberweisung',FALSE);
      InsertPaymentType('15','Intern. StandardÅberweisung unterhalb d. Meldegrenze',FALSE);
      InsertPaymentType('20','Scheckziehung,Versandform freigestellt',TRUE);
      InsertPaymentType('21','Scheckziehung,Versandform per Einschreiben',TRUE);
      InsertPaymentType('22','Scheckziehung,Versandform per Eilboten',TRUE);
      InsertPaymentType('23','Scheckziehung,Versandform per Einschreiben/Eilboten',TRUE);
      InsertPaymentType('30','Scheckziehung an Auftraggeber, Versandform freigestellt',TRUE);
      InsertPaymentType('31','Scheckziehung an Auftraggeber, Versandform Einschreiben',TRUE);
      InsertPaymentType('32','Scheckziehung an Auftraggeber, Versandform Eilboten',TRUE);
      InsertPaymentType('33','Scheckziehung an Auftraggeber, Versandform Einschreiben/Eilboten',TRUE);
    END;

    PROCEDURE InsertBBC@1105400018(BLZCode@1105400000 : Code[20];BLZBankname@1105400001 : Text[100];BLZCity@1105400002 : Text[100]);
    BEGIN
      BankCode.Code := BLZCode;
      BankCode."Bank Name" := COPYSTR(BLZBankname,1,MAXSTRLEN(BankCode."Bank Name"));
      BankCode.City := COPYSTR(BLZCity,1,MAXSTRLEN(BankCode.City));

      CASE Mode OF
        Mode::Ins : BankCode.INSERT;
        Mode::Skip : IF NOT BankCode.INSERT THEN ;
        Mode::Modify: IF NOT BankCode.INSERT THEN BankCode.MODIFY;
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE InsertTextCode@1105400019(TextCodeStr@1105400000 : Code[3];Text@1105400001 : Text[80]);
    BEGIN
      TextCode.Code := TextCodeStr;
      TextCode.Description := Text;

      CASE Mode OF
        Mode::Ins : TextCode.INSERT;
        Mode::Skip : IF NOT TextCode.INSERT THEN ;
        Mode::Modify: IF NOT TextCode.INSERT THEN TextCode.MODIFY;
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE InsertRights@1105400020(Type@1105400000 : Integer;ID@1105400001 : Integer;Read@1105400002 : Integer;Insert@1105400003 : Integer;Modify@1105400004 : Integer;Delete@1105400005 : Integer;Run@1105400006 : Integer);
    BEGIN
      Access.VALIDATE("Role ID",AccessName);
      Access.VALIDATE("Object Type", Type);
      Access.VALIDATE("Object ID",ID);
      Access.VALIDATE("Read Permission", Read);
      Access.VALIDATE("Insert Permission", Insert);
      Access.VALIDATE("Modify Permission", Modify);
      Access.VALIDATE("Delete Permission", Delete);
      Access.VALIDATE("Execute Permission", Run);

      CASE Mode OF
        Mode::Ins : Access.INSERT;
        Mode::Skip : IF NOT Access.INSERT THEN ;
        Mode::Modify: IF NOT Access.INSERT THEN Access.MODIFY;
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE InsertBankInterfaceField@1105400028(Code@1105400000 : Code[10];EntryNo@1105400001 : Integer;FNo@1105400002 : Integer;FFactor@1105400003 : Decimal);
    BEGIN
      BankInterfaceField."Bank Interface Code" := Code;
      BankInterfaceField."Entry No." := EntryNo;
      BankInterfaceField."Fieldno." := FNo;
      BankInterfaceField.Factor := FFactor;
      IF NOT BankInterfaceField.INSERT THEN;
    END;

    PROCEDURE InsertPaymentArea@1105400031(Code@1105400000 : Code[10];Description@1105400001 : Text[70]);
    BEGIN
      PaymentArea.Code := Code;
      PaymentArea.Description := Description;

      CASE Mode OF
        Mode::Ins : PaymentArea.INSERT;
        Mode::Skip : IF NOT PaymentArea.INSERT THEN ;
        Mode::Modify: IF NOT PaymentArea.INSERT THEN PaymentArea.MODIFY;
      END;
    END;

    BEGIN
    END.
